Speaking of reusing items, Level 75: The Gallium Caves is a great place to reuse both the LIDAR Scanner and the Temperature Detector thing. How Level 88 works is that you are trapped in a cave made all of gallium. Each section can heat up or cool down. Since each section is made entirely of gallium, if you are stuck in a melting section, you will eventually drown in the melting gallium. Some parts of the level could also be too dark for a flashlight, and that's where the LIDAR scanner comes in.

8:54 â€œI still have TONS of plans for this game like adding even more official levelsâ€  these levels havenâ€™t been official this whole time?
I'm making a procedural world generator for the backrooms in minecraft. I definitely came up with some great methods for this. very good performance and a good distribution of big and small rooms with all kinds of weird shapes. I've been working on this for 2 and a half years now. it's getting closer to finished. if you use anything I made, credit would be appreciated. it's called pxnBackrooms. there is a lite version which only has level 0 and the code is much simpler. the full plugin has 14 different levels at the moment (not including sublevels) and I have another 25 levels planned. it has been a fun project.

Level -1. Class 2.  Level -1 is a presumably infinite hallway that has doors on either side. The Level consists of white-painted walls and numerous black doors. Each door leads to either level -2, level 0, The whiteout or Level 2. Whilst inside this Level, one will no longer hear the hum-buzz of Level 0. Instead, one may hear slight piano noises in the distance; the source of the sound is unknown. The deeper one traverses through this Level, the slightly louder it gets, but it never seems to get any closer. Your vision seems to get more static-like effects while walking too far down the hall. During this time, you can hear some old advertisements from around the 1930's era through the static noise. Soon, your vision becomes black and white with the static effect. While this event plays out, you can see people in old business suits, although their human features are completely invisible to the human eye, the only thing visible is their attire. You may also hear the chatter of many beings mixed with the sounds previously mentioned. Almond water puddles can also be found on the floor during this event, dripping from the ceiling.  Credit to the backrooms wiki page.  Also IMPORTANT don't over work yourself I've realised most developers get something named burnout its where you get too stressed to do Anything. So I recommend to take a break after maybe like 2 updates although its up to you.

Level -1. Class 2.  Level -1 is a presumably infinite hallway that has doors on either side. The Level consists of white-painted walls and numerous black doors. Each door leads to eitherÂ level -2,Â level 0,Â The whiteoutÂ orÂ Level 2. Whilst inside this Level, one will no longer hear the hum-buzz ofÂ Level 0. Instead, one may hear slight piano noises in the distance; the source of the sound is unknown. The deeper one traverses through this Level, the slightly louder it gets, but it never seems to get any closer. Your vision seems to get more static-like effects while walking too far down the hall. During this time, you can hear some old advertisements from around the 1930's era through the static noise. Soon, your vision becomes black and white with the static effect. While this event plays out, you can see people in old business suits, although their human features are completely invisible to the human eye, the only thing visible is their attire. You may also hear the chatter of many beings mixed with the sounds previously mentioned.Â Almond waterÂ puddles can also be found on the floor during this event, dripping from the ceiling. how would i play this game now im afraid of butterflies
I have a problem with the smilers now being just faces in the dark. They're simply not scary anymore. Their faces get on top of the lights from the other safe rooms very often and, not only that, you can use a flashlight on them to see that they are just faces, the light goes through them. Also, their former spider appearance really worked, because you couldn't see them fully, but some of their parts were visible when they were near your room and your brain did the rest of the job. I suggest you give them back their spider appearance but make them not visible in the flashlight, just like they're not visible when the lights are on, even if there's only a tiny part getting in the view. This will work well for their creepiness. Or if you really want to keep them as faces, make them not visible when they get on top of the lights from the other rooms and when the flashlight is used on them. The other suggestion is simply not giving the player a flashlight before they finish level 1. Also, I feel really weird about these random generations. Pre set, but well executed linear experience is perfectly well, and I really enjoyed the game. Just maybe make the hotel 'Look up' stage bigger, because while I absolutely love everything about this level, it felt more like a normal hotel with less than 30 rooms, the only difference being two entities roaming the halls. The level is good, but just make the map a bit more complicated. Also, I think it would be a great idea for the numbers of the rooms to be completely random 3-digits so that it's not that easy to remember where is the room you need to find. It would also really add to the atmosphere and make you truly feel like you're in the backrooms, despite the level being a bit too small. Back to the topic, maybe you can make like 10 or 15 different versions of every stage for the replayability and a random one will appear on every playthrough. The problem with completely randomized levels is that most likely the game will not be balanced. Finding an exit to a level might get ridiculously difficult and a lot of enemy placements might turn out very unfair. Not gonna lie, I would love it if the levels were bigger, but randomizing everything would lead to massive problems that might destroy all the fun and make the game frustrating

Suggestion: Entity 666 If you don't know what entity 666 is, it is an entity that appears in any level with a computer. It disguises itself ss an exe file and when you try to download it, mistaking it for a game, it will appear in whatever game you tried to download and track you down ingame. Once it reaches you, it will jumpscare you. Then, it shuts off all the lights in your room and then it will manifest itself into a living being and proceed to jumpscare you untill you have a heart attack, If that doesn't work, it will kill you in an incredibly gory way and then delete itself and any evidence of it ever existing, and then waits for another victim to get. You can make it so you can go on the computers where you can play a game to get a big hint or a tool or something. There are 5 options and 3 are Entity 666, if you choose the wrong one, he will appear and kill you.
